Zhenjiang

Measures for Depositing and Remitting Public Funds in Various Counties: The Jiangsu Farmers Bank has established the following measures for depositing and remitting public funds in various counties, as stipulated by the Supervisory Committee: (1) In counties where the Farmers Bank has established branches but there are no agencies acting as the provincial treasury, all local and provincial public funds of the county shall be deposited in the Farmers Bank, and the Farmers Bank shall be the agency for receiving and remitting public funds. (2) If the deposit interest rate of local county funds is equal to or less than the interest rate of the Farmers Bank, the county's assets office may still deposit them elsewhere. (3) The Farmers Bank may charge remittance fees or handling fees for public funds entrusted to it by agencies for collection and remittance. (4) If agencies depositing funds in the Farmers Bank urgently need funds and are temporarily unable to turn around, they may pledge their deposit books to the Farmers Bank to apply for loans, but the maximum loan amount shall not exceed 90% of the amount in the deposit book.

Construction Engineering Office Sets Deadline for Grave Relocations: The Provincial Capital Construction Engineering Office has now decided to build a road from the North Gate to Beigushan and will begin construction soon. The land needed on both sides of the road has already been demarcated by the office. However, there are many graves in the open spaces on both sides, and if they are not relocated, it will hinder the work. Yesterday, a notice was issued, informing all grave owners in the area to relocate by June 25th. If they fail to relocate by the deadline, the graves will be treated as ownerless and relocated by the Red Swastika Society to facilitate the progress of the work. The Provincial Government Plans to Issue Salaries for the Security Regiment: The Jiangsu Provincial Government urgently needed to issue salaries for the security regiment but the treasury was empty and there was no way to transfer funds. It specially borrowed 150,000 yuan each from the Chambers of Commerce of Zhenjiang, Wuxi, and Suzhou, using business tax revenue as collateral. Currently, the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce has borrowed 60,000 yuan, the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce has borrowed 30,000 yuan, but the Suzhou Chamber of Commerce has not yet agreed to lend the money.

Jiang-Zhe Provinces Jointly Suppress Bandits in Taihu Lake: The governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces, because of the rampant bandits in Taihu Lake on the border of the two provinces, discussed methods of joint suppression. A Joint Bandit Suppression Command Headquarters for Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces was specially established in Suzhou, and Zhu Mian, the commander of the Jiangsu Security Department, was appointed as the chief commander, and Wang Zhiqi, the commander of the Zhejiang Security Department, was appointed as the deputy commander, responsible for the suppression. It is learned that the chief and deputy commanders have taken office and are working, and have drafted a bandit suppression plan, which has been submitted to the Jiangsu Pacification Superintendent's Office for adoption and implementation. The areas for bandit suppression are as follows: (1) Twenty-six villages in Wujiang County: Shengze, Maogang, Sitingzhi, Miaoqian, Damiaogang, Lujiagang, Nanku, Caogang, Jinze, Qiligang, Sidu, Lima Jiadang, Wu Lou Tangqian, Nan Canggang, Jiu Xi Gang, Mao Zi Gang, Zhi Du Gang, Lie Que Kou, Pan Qi Gang, Yu Gang, Zhang Qi Miao Gang, and Po Che Gang, Hengta; (2) Eight locations in Changxing County: Lushan, Bai Fubu, Xiao Chengdu, Xintang, Shuikou, Li Jia Gang, Da Wu Shan, Xiao Wu Shan; (3) Ten locations in Wuxing County: Cangshan, Bian Shan Chang, Qing Cao Hu, Zhong Zhao, Xin Xing Gang, Shi Cong, Song Lou, Hu Quan, Yi Gao, and Jia Pu. The joint suppression period is tentatively set for one and a half months to eliminate the major bandit forces. The situation will be observed temporarily, and the period may be extended as appropriate. A division or more of troops will be dispatched, advancing on both land and water routes.

Further Details on the Robbery of Two Small Steamships by Bandits: Regarding the robbery of the Dada Company's Dattai steamship towing the Feipeng boat, and the Jiangtai Company's Taiheng steamship towing the No. 5 boat, on the same day at Gudianpu, fifty miles from Yancheng, by bandit boats, a friend of the company recounted the incident, saying that after the bandits robbed the two company steamships, they also damaged the machinery of the small steamships. Subsequently, the company's Taizhou branch sent a ship to tow them to Yancheng, reported to the authorities for inspection. It was also learned that Yang Hanshi, the accountant of Dada, was struck in the back. Because the Jiangtai ship was worth a thousand yuan, he could not care about anything else. Therefore, the accountant Zhang Liangcai was spared from being attacked.

The Provincial Committee Urgently Requests Loans from the Chamber of Commerce: Chuan Zhiren, a member of the Provincial Committee, came to Yangzhou on the 17th to urgently request that the County Chamber of Commerce recognize and borrow 5,000 yuan in business tax funds. Gaoyou

Detailed Record of the Trial of the Case of Seducing a Young Girl: Xiao Cunzi, the daughter of Chang Tianshun, a merchant in Lingqiao Town in this county, was previously seduced by Yang Xipeng, a neighbor. Now that the wedding date is approaching, Yang hid the girl at home, preparing to elope with her the next morning. This was discovered by the girl's father, who reported it to the Public Security Office. Officer Song led police to arrest the pair of lovebirds and send them to the county government. At 9:00 PM on the 15th, Trial Judge Ji held a trial. According to Chang Tianshun's testimony, he is 60 years old, lives in Lingqiao Town, works as a merchant, and has two daughters. The eldest daughter is already married. Xiao Cunzi is my second daughter and is engaged to someone. She is 19 years old this year, with her birthday in October. I don't know when she had a relationship with Yang Xipeng. On the evening of the 25th of this month according to the lunar calendar, she suddenly took away a gold hairpin, a gold ring, and a bank note for 80 yuan. Later, I investigated and found out that she had fled to Yang's house. I went to look for her, but Yang Xipeng threatened me with a pistol. So I reported to the Public Security Substation. Officer Song led the police to search his house and found the opium paraphernalia and bullets. According to Xiao Cunzi's testimony, she is 19 years old, with her birthday in October. She has had a relationship with Yang Xipeng for four months, more than a dozen times in total, all at his house. He usually smokes opium. On the evening of the 25th, he tricked me into going to his house. I brought a gold hairpin, a gold ring, and a bank note for 80 yuan. Later, I wanted to go home, but he threatened me with a pistol and wouldn't let me go home. He has already taken away the gold ring. According to witnesses Chang Hucun, village official Xia Mingde, and Xiao Cunzi's uncle Xue Fengchao, their testimonies are the same as Chang Shuntian's. According to Yang Xipeng's testimony, he is 31 years old, lives in Lingqiao Town, and is in the education field. He previously served in the general affairs section of the Administrative Bureau. I have not had a relationship with Xiao Cunzi. I don't smoke opium, and I don't have a pistol, only a shotgun for self-defense, and I have a gun license. On the evening of the 25th, I was wandering on the street and heard that someone was searching my house. I was very surprised and went home. I saw Xiao Cunzi inside my house. I asked her what she was doing there. She said she was borrowing rice and heard someone shouting and making noise outside, afraid it was bandits, so she hid here. At that time, Officer Song suddenly came with the police to arrest me. I don't know about the guns, bullets, and opium paraphernalia. Chang Tianshun has a grudge against me and is trying to harm me. After the interrogation, Chang Tianshun was ordered to sign a guarantee to take Xiao Cunzi back and strictly supervise her. Yang Xipeng was detained first.

Funing

Ninth District Actively Controls Locusts: The Ninth District of Funing County has mostly beach land, which is traditionally a locust-producing area. Currently, due to the drought, locust nymphs have been discovered successively. The district's Pest Control Team has telegraphed the county government and reported to the Coastal Locust Control Office. Mr. Shen Yaozhi, the locust control commissioner stationed in Funing, was requested to supervise the capture. Subsequently, Sun Deyuan, the chairman of the Locust Control Association, personally went to the district to coordinate the prevention and control efforts with Zhao Wenzhi, the head of the Pest Control Team, and others. They supervised the capture in different directions and inspected the beaches all day long. The initial discovery site has been cleared, and efforts are being made to supervise the capture in other areas.

Ship Lock Company Collects Additional 20%: The county government, based on a report from the Education Bureau, forwarded it to the Department of Education regarding the Tangzha Zesheng Ship Lock Company collecting an additional 20% for education fees to offset overdue fines. The Department of Education consulted the Department of Finance, which replied that the education fee is collected based on the original fee standard and is not a tax on goods. It does not increase the burden on ship owners, and the company has agreed to it. It is feasible. The county government was instructed to inform the company and to quickly draft simple regulations for the additional collection, submit them for approval, and submit them to the provincial government for discussion and implementation.

Registering Field Mu Based on Land Survey Records: He Liangyu, the land tax commissioner of the Department of Finance, believes that if the registered number of mu of fields is based solely on the deeds provided by the owners, it may still be inaccurate. He specifically requested that the Land Tax Investigation Committee decide that the registration of fields should be based on the number of mu recorded in the land survey maps and registers, and issue a notice requiring all owners to present their grain strings and land survey vouchers for verification during registration.

Troops Assist with Agricultural Work: The 280th Regiment of the National Army stationed in Tongzhou is quite concerned about the suffering of the local people. Now that wheat has ripened and it is time to plant soybeans, hemp, cotton, and rice, impoverished rural farmers often suffer from a lack of livestock to assist with farming, making cultivation particularly difficult. On the 18th, Regiment Commander Pan specially issued a notice stating that all of the regiment's hundred or so mules and horses were available for poor farmers to borrow to assist with agricultural work and expand planting.

The Start of Steamship Service on the City-Lianghu Canal: The waterway from the county seat to Lianghu in the western countryside is about thirty li. Hefei

Relief for the Unprecedented Fire: According to detailed investigations after the unprecedented fire the other day, more than 370 businesses were burned, with more than 740 main and subsidiary households, and losses exceeding 2 million. About 8,000 to 9,000 houses were destroyed. Because thousands of disaster victims were sleeping in the open without food, which was truly pitiful, the Red Swastika Society started distributing bread and congee on the 13th. On the 14th, due to heavy rain, the disaster victims had nowhere to shelter, so the Red Swastika Society, the Siguxiang Puyi Society, and the Christian Agricultural and Forestry Farm were urgently prepared as shelters for male and female disaster victims. However, due to the large number of people and limited funds, food was only supplied for one week. In the afternoon of the 14th, people from all walks of life held a meeting at the Chamber of Commerce to organize a fire emergency relief committee. More than a hundred people, including Yang Litsuo, Liu Junyao, and Xu Ketang, were designated as committee members for the five districts: east, west, south, north, and central. Donations for relief began on the 15th. County Magistrate Zhang Shusen also telegraphed the province to report the fire and request relief.

Recent News on Liu Yuanchi's Detention: Liu Yuanchi, the editor-in-chief of the Minguo Daily, was imprisoned last month for publishing an article about a soldier and the county court clerk colluding to transport land. It has been more than a month. The Minguo Daily and the Minbao have separately accused the provincial government and the high court of bending the law for personal gain, protecting opium dealers, and illegally detaining him and suppressing freedom of speech. The provincial government has now decided to work with the high court to send personnel to Feihe to thoroughly investigate the matter and has telegraphed to approve his bail.

Education News　Important News

Ministry of Education Increases Primary School Teachers' Salaries

▲Formulate the Lowest and Highest Salary Measures

Nanjing, 19th telegram: The Ministry of Education is drafting a plan to increase the salaries of primary school teachers. Currently, the level of social life has increased. The salaries of middle school teachers are used to determine the minimum standard for primary school teachers' salaries to ensure that they can maintain their livelihoods. Second, the maximum amount of primary school teachers' salaries is stipulated, based on the teacher's academic qualifications, experience, and performance as the standard, and an annual salary increase system is implemented until the maximum amount is reached.

Zhejiang Education Expenses Have Been Settled, and the Department Head Returns to Office

▲The Ministry of Education Advises the Zhejiang Provincial Government to Stop the Activities of the Education Federation

It was previously reported that Zhang Daofan, the head of the Zhejiang Department of Education, repeatedly submitted his resignation, but the Ministry and other departments repeatedly ordered him to stay, and middle school teachers and staff telegraphed requesting that Jian be appointed as the successor department head, but the Ministry of Education rejected this. Subsequently, the Finance Department allocated the overdue expenses for each month of this year. The Ministry of Education has ordered Zhang Daofan to return to office, and the Zhejiang Provincial Middle School Teachers and Staff Federation has sent another telegram to the Ministry. The Ministry of Education believes that Zhang Daofan's active planning has been quite successful. In addition to ordering Zhang Daofan to return to office, the Ministry also considered the illegal activities of the Education Federation and immediately advised the Zhejiang Provincial Government to order the association to end its activities as soon as possible. The order is recorded below:

▲Order to Zhang Daofan: This Ministry previously received a report from the Department Head requesting that his concurrent positions be removed. It was instructed to retain him, and the State Council of the Executive Yuan resolved to retain him. Subsequently, the Department Head submitted a report reiterating the previous request. At that time, the Ministry advised the Zhejiang Provincial Government to raise and allocate the accumulated education expenses and ordered him to continue in his full-time position and not resign again. Now that the Zhejiang Province has allocated the accumulated education expenses for each month of this year, the Department Head's planned projects can be gradually advanced. He should continue to work hard to complete the task. Therefore, he is ordered to return to the Department immediately and carefully plan and actively carry out all educational facilities in Zhejiang Province, thereby fulfilling the Ministry's earnest expectations.

▲Advisory to the Zhejiang Provincial Government: This Ministry previously received a report from Zhang Daofan, the head of the Zhejiang Department of Education, requesting that his concurrent positions be removed. It was instructed to retain him, and the State Council of the Executive Yuan resolved to retain him. The Ministry also advised your government to find ways to raise and allocate accumulated education expenses to maintain operations. Now that the accumulated education expenses in Zhejiang Province have been allocated by your government, the Department Head should return to the Department immediately and continue to work hard to complete the task. He has been ordered to comply. However, it was found that teachers and staff of Provincial Second, Sixth, and Tenth Middle Schools have telegraphed at different times, stating that Zhang Daofan, the head of the Zhejiang Department of Education, has resigned and requesting that a successor be appointed as soon as possible. The appointment of the Department Head is at the discretion of the central government, and the request is inappropriate and has been rejected. Recently, a telegram was sent to the Ministry in the name of the Zhejiang Provincial Middle School Teachers and Staff Federation, presenting the same situation as before. It has been found that the teachers and staff are interfering with the selection of educational administrative officials even after the government has issued an explicit order to retain him, which is absurd. This Ministry previously approved a letter from the Central Training Department stating that the Jiangxi Provincial Middle and Higher Education Teachers and Staff Federation had no legal basis and was considered an illegal organization, and ordered the Jiangxi Department of Education to stop the association's activities and instructed them to handle its dissolution. The situation of the Zhejiang Provincial Middle School Teachers and Staff Federation is the same and should be handled in the same way. Your government is advised to investigate, promptly stop the association's activities, and order it to dissolve in accordance with the law. We hope you will inform us of the handling situation. Sincere respects.

Junior High School Credits Revised to 180-183

Industrial Arts Renamed Manual Arts

Civics Not Offered in Senior and Junior High Schools

丨Decision Made Yesterday by the Middle School Group of the Curriculum Standards and Equipment Compilation Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools丨

Nanjing, 19th telegram: The middle school group of the Curriculum Standards and Equipment Compilation Committee for Primary and Secondary Schools met at the Ministry of Education at 9:00 AM on the 19th. Attendees included Xu Yuanqi, Zheng Tonghe, Gu Shusen, Wu Yan'yin, etc., chaired by Gu Shusen. The meeting discussed the Ministry of Education's opinions on the middle school curriculum standards and decided: 1. Civics will not be added to senior and junior high schools. The method of supplementing civics teaching materials will be determined by a committee appointed by this meeting to submit opinions and send them to the Standing Committee for examination when reviewing Party principles. 2. The total number of junior high school credits will be revised to 180-183, with physical education, the Party, and Boy Scouts accounting for 15 credits, and other subjects accounting for 165-168 credits. 3. The distribution of new credits for junior high school will be changed as follows: Party Principles: 12 credits (original standard), Chinese: 38, Foreign Language: 30 (required in the third year), History: 9 (Chinese History: 6, Foreign History: 3), Geography: 9 (Chinese Geography: 6, Foreign Geography: 3), Mathematics: 28, Natural Science: 15, Physiology and Hygiene: 3, Drawing: 4, Music: 4, Physical Education, Party, and Boy Scouts: 15, Industrial Arts renamed Manual Arts: 9, Elective Subjects: 4-7. 4. The order of subjects in the junior high school curriculum should be re-determined. The primary school group held a subcommittee review meeting on the 19th and will continue to hold a second general meeting on the afternoon of the 20th.

Another report states that the primary school group decided the other day regarding the "Party Principles Issue in Primary Schools." The original resolution was: "The Central Training Department advocates that Party Principles should not be specifically offered as a subject in primary schools. If the Central Government formally decides, then various teaching materials related to Party Principles should be incorporated into various subjects. The method of incorporation will be determined by the subject review committees."

Black Star Amateur Basketball Team of the Municipal First Stadium Wins the Championship Without Effort

▲Sheguang Forfeits Due to Only One Player Arriving

The amateur basketball competition of the Municipal First Public Stadium, Group A, Black Star vs. Sheguang Two teams, the final decisive match was yesterday at 5:50 PM. In the morning, it rained, and Sheguang and Black Star inquired by telephone whether the match would be held or not. The reply was that the rain would stop in the afternoon, and the match would be held immediately. The venue was being paved with sand for renovation. According to the regulations, whether or not the match is held in the event of rain must be determined by the inquiry committee. In the afternoon, the rain did stop, and the venue was able to be used for combat after being renovated. Black Star team members were geared up to fight, while only one member from Sheguang arrived. There were not enough players to play a game. Ten minutes passed, and still no more players showed up. The referee Zhang Longhai then announced that Sheguang forfeited. Thus, the Black Star team won the Group A championship without any effort.

Wu Yijun, Saigon's All-Around Table Tennis Champion, Arrives in Shanghai

▲Arrived Yesterday from Hong Kong and Lodges at Zhonghe Foreign Firm

Wu Yijun, former secretary and table tennis coach of the Nansing Sports Association in Saigon (from Zhongshan, Guangdong), has now arrived in Shanghai from Hong Kong and is staying at the residence of his brother Wu Yaohao, a compradore at Zhonghe Foreign Firm. Mr. Wu has many friends in Shanghai, all of whom have returned from Japan. Mr. Wu's ball skills are purely of the Japanese style, so he is good at attacking, and he is particularly unique in drawing the ball. Mr. Shimizu, a famous Japanese player (former first place in Japan), knows him very well. Some friends want to take the opportunity of Mr. Wu's visit to Shanghai to introduce him to sea-based athletes and put on a table tennis friendly performance, but Mr. Wu is very humble, saying that he is tired from the journey and physically unwell, and his ball skills have deteriorated to the extreme, and he is not what he used to be, and he does not want to show his ugliness, please wait for another day, etc.

Record of the South Manchuria Railway International Games (1)

丨Opening Ceremony of the South Manchuria Railway International Stadium丨Participants from China, Japan, and Russia丨

▲Dongda Wins Football Championship丨Yu Xiwei Sets New Record in Long Distance Running

(Shenyang Correspondence) The opening ceremony and opening commemorative sports meeting of the International Sports Field built by the South Manchuria Railway Co., Ltd. of Japan were held on the 13th and 14th. In addition to track and field events, there were three events: football, volleyball, and baseball. The weather was fine after the overnight rain. Before the venue, the national flags of China, the United Kingdom, the United States, Russia, France, and other countries fluttered in the wind, creating a lively atmosphere. As a result of the sports, Northeastern University won the football championship, and Yu Xiwei, a student of Fengyong University, set a special record in the 800-meter and 1,500-meter races. The details are as follows:

Unparalleled Magnificent Arrangement

The sports field is a curtain wall type, all built with reinforced concrete. The competition field is 400 meters around, with an area of 4,400 meters. It can be opened as a skating rink in winter. The whole field can accommodate 9,000 spectators. The stands are tiered, and the facilities in each room include male and female athletes' rooms, shower rooms, changing rooms, rest rooms, offices, preparation rooms, sales rooms, and toilets, totaling 35 rooms. The construction cost was 136,000 Japanese yen. Construction began in June last year and was completed at the end of November. Now the equipment is perfect.

Unprecedented Grand Opening

At 9 o'clock, a cannon was fired to start the meeting. The officials of the conference were lined up in the field to hold the purification ceremony, which lasted 20 minutes. Next, the flag was raised and music was played. Director Omori of the South Manchuria Railway delivered a speech on behalf of President Sengoku, which roughly meant that the South Manchuria Railway Company, in view of the development of sports undertakings in various countries, as an element of integrating international feelings, built a large-scale international sports field in Shenyang, the central location of the Northeast. The construction of the project has been completed, and today the opening commemoration is held and a sports competition is held. I am deeply honored that you have come. This sports field is not only equipped for students, but also hopes that the public at home and abroad will come to practice sports and temper their bodies. After the speech, the athletes were organized into teams and lined up in the center of the venue. (1) Volleyball team: Tongze Girls' High School, Northeastern University, Northeastern Student Team; (2) Football team: Northeastern Student Team, Fengyong University; (3) Volleyball team: Fengnu High School, All Dalian Team, Medical University; (4) Football team: All Dalian, Medical University; (5) Baseball team: Andong, Fushun, Changchun, and Fengtian four major teams. Then, under the command of Shikagawa and the guidance of Kigu, they paraded around the venue for half a week. The Japanese attendees were all representatives of the inland along the line.

Zhang Zuoxiang, Zang Shiyi, Rong Zhen, and others did not attend due to business, but Chen Wenxue, Wang Jinghuan, Zhao Xinbo, Ning Encheng, Feng Yong, Tao Shangming, Cao Chengzong, and other dignitaries attended, and Consul General Lin and others also attended as escorts.

The Yu Da Collides with a British Vessel

▲ Official Report Released

Following the collision between the Haichang Shipping Company's Yu Da vessel and the British vessel Peston, the Yu Da has arrived in Shanghai. After inspection by surveyors, it was found that over ten rivets on the bow need to be replaced. Due to rain yesterday, repairs have not yet commenced. If the weather clears today, repairs will be carried out, and the vessel should sail this afternoon. The official report from the captain following the collision, along with the translated text of the signed exchange document between the two captains, are detailed below:

▲ Translation of the Yu Da Captain's Report: This is a report regarding the facts of the case of the collision between the Yu Da vessel and the British submarine Peston (transliteration) on June 9, 1931. The Yu Da vessel departed Shanghai for Niuzhuang on June 7, carrying 1,050 tons of mixed cargo. The vessel's draft was 13 feet 1 inch forward and 15 feet 1 inch aft. On the morning of June 9, after passing the Shandong Cape Lighthouse, the Yu Da vessel's course was 42 degrees northwest. At approximately noon, a submarine was sighted on the vessel's starboard side, floating motionless. The Yu Da vessel continued on its course. As it approached, the submarine was seen to engage its propellers and move forward, crossing the Yu Da's path from starboard to port. I assessed that the angle between the submarine and the Yu Da remained almost unchanged, and the distance between the two vessels was closing rapidly. In order to avoid a collision, in accordance with Articles 19 and 22 of the International Regulations for Preventing Collisions at Sea (Article 19 states that when two vessels are approaching each other head-on or nearly head-on, and one vessel sees the other on her starboard side, she shall keep out of the way of the other to avoid collision; Article 22 states that any vessel which is required to keep out of the way of another shall, so far as possible, take positive early action to comply with this obligation, and shall, if the circumstances of the case admit, avoid crossing ahead of the other vessel), I immediately turned the helm to starboard to give way, intending to pass behind the submarine, and sounded one short blast on the whistle. During this time, my actions were as described above. When the two vessels were very close, the submarine suddenly changed course and moved back from the vessel's port side to starboard. This imminent danger of collision was solely due to the submarine's unexpected maneuver. For safety reasons, I immediately engaged full astern, sounding three short blasts on the whistle, and turned the helm hard over. However, at 12:12 PM on June 9, the midship section of the submarine's starboard side collided with the bow of the Yu Da vessel. The location of the collision was at 37 degrees 43 minutes north latitude and 122 degrees 16 minutes east longitude. The weather at the time was fair but not very clear, with visibility of approximately four nautical miles. After the collision, I immediately stopped the engines and sounded the distress signal, using all possible means to assist the submarine's crew. The submarine quickly sank. After searching the area, a total of 25 survivors were rescued and transferred to the submarine's supply ship. At 5:12 PM, after another British warship arrived at the scene, the Yu Da departed for Niuzhuang, arriving at 6:00 PM on the 10th. The bow of the Yu Da sustained minor damage. Yu Da Captain, Jia Shi Zhongzhong.

▲ Translation of the Signed Exchange Document Between the Two Captains: (1) Letter from the Yu Da Captain to the Submarine Captain: At noon, the submarine was sighted on the Yu Da's starboard side at a distance of approximately four nautical miles. The Yu Da's course was 42 degrees northwest. At 12:08, the bearing of the submarine was measured to be three points (34 degrees) on the Yu Da's starboard side, at a distance of two nautical miles. At 12:10, the submarine began to move forward. At 12:11:45, the Yu Da engaged full astern. The captain was on the bridge. At 12:12, the two vessels collided. The weather at the time was fair but unclear, with visibility of approximately four nautical miles. Yu Da shipowner, signature.

(2) Letter from the Submarine Captain to the Yu Da Captain: The submarine surfaced and remained stationary at 11:45 AM, with its bow pointing southwest. At 12:04, the Yu Da vessel was sighted on the submarine's port side, at a distance of approximately 1,500 yards, heading approximately northwest, three points to the right of the submarine. The submarine began moving forward and turned to port at 12:05, sounding one blast on the whistle. Before the Yu Da vessel turned to starboard, the distance between the two vessels was approximately 1,200 yards. At 12:09, the Yu Da was seen turning to starboard. I sounded two more blasts on the whistle. The submarine's course was 10 degrees south of east. The collision occurred at 12:12. The submarine's bow was heading due east, and the Yu Da's bow was heading approximately due north. The two vessels collided at right angles. The weather was cloudy and calm, with visibility of six nautical miles. Submarine Captain, signature.

The Municipal Social Bureau Establishes a Station to Purchase Rice Stem Borer Eggs and Moths

Rice stem borers are a pest to rice, as everyone knows. The Municipal Social Bureau has spared no effort over the years in preventing and eliminating rice stem borers, dispatching personnel to various districts to provide practical guidance, organizing cooperative stem borer removal experiments, and establishing a station to purchase stem borer eggs and moths, all of which have been quite effective in promoting awareness. Rice fields in various districts have now been planted with seedlings several inches long. All the stem borers are hatching one after another, sucking up nutrients and harming the rice crop. If precautions are not taken and problems are nipped in the bud, the future transformations will be unbearable. In view of this, the Bureau, in addition to repeatedly ordering the municipal committee members of each district to assist farmers within their boundaries in working hard to eliminate the pests and earnestly prevent them, has also formulated strict measures to dig up rice roots and recently formulated methods for searching and catching stem borers, which have been successively announced to farmers in the urban area for compliance and implementation. However, the villagers are poorly educated and have weak financial resources. It is heard that the Bureau, in order to awaken the farmers' efforts to search and catch the pests, in order to enrich people's food, is still setting up a station to purchase stem borer eggs and moths according to last year's method. The price is temporarily set at one copper coin for every two stem borer eggs and moths. The Bureau's purchasing methods are recorded below:

▲ Methods for Purchasing Rice Stem Borer Eggs and Moths: 1. The Bureau will establish a station to purchase rice stem borer eggs and moths in areas of the city where stem borer damage is more severe, in order to achieve the purpose of preventing and eliminating stem borers and enriching people's food. 2. The Bureau's purchasing stations will be temporarily established in six locations: Yinhang, Wusong, Tangqiao, Gaoxing, Caojing, and the Municipal Agricultural Experiment Station. 3. Each purchasing station will be headed by one director, concurrently held by the municipal committee members of each district and the director of the agricultural experiment station, who will be responsible for all matters of the station. Purchasing staff will be concurrently held by the staff of the district municipal committee office and the experiment station. 4. The Bureau will, at its discretion, provide subsidies based on the work ethic and the number of acquisitions of each purchasing station. 5. Each purchasing station should report any special circumstances to the Bureau for approval at any time. 6. Purchasing stations are under the guidance and supervision of the Bureau. 7. The purchased stem borer eggs and moths, together with the weekly report form, should be submitted to the Bureau for verification and cancellation before 2:00 PM every Monday. 8. When farmers sell stem borer eggs and moths, they should first tie ten egg masses into a bundle and seal ten moths in a bag to facilitate easy counting. 9. The purchasing price will be set by the Bureau and announced to each purchasing station at any time. 10. The purchasing time is set from 8:00 AM to 4:00 PM daily. 11. The purchasing period is set to end at the end of August, and may be extended at the discretion of the Bureau if necessary. 12. These measures will be implemented from the date of publication.

Qin Runqing Discusses the Money Shop Law

▲ Still Hoping the Government Will Enact Separate Regulations

Regarding the request of the money industry to enact separate money shop laws, the Legislative Yuan decided that there was no need to enact separate special legislation and that it could be supplemented in the Banking Law Enforcement Regulations in the future. Yesterday, a reporter from the New Voice News Agency interviewed Qin Runqing, a leader in the money industry, about this matter and asked for his opinion. According to him, banks and money shops are essentially very different in nature. Banks mainly provide loans with collateral, while money shops mainly provide loans based on credit. Although banks also provide credit loans and money shops also provide mortgage loans, these are in the minority. Banks are all limited liability organizations, while money shops bear unlimited liability. Furthermore, the minimum capital of banks is set at 500,000, while the largest capital of the more than 70 exchange money shops in this city is only 400,000 to 500,000, and most are around 100,000, while the annual business is more than 700,000 to 800,000. Therefore, shareholders must make advances at any time and cannot predetermine the amount. In the money shops of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, the capital is mostly 5,000 or 10,000, while the annual business is also hundreds of thousands. Banks have a history of at most 40 to 50 years, while money shops have a history of 300 to 400 years. Mr. Ma Yinchu is a banker and is inevitably out of touch with money shops. His opinions may be based on one-sided observations. I still hope that the government will enact separate money shop laws. Now, after the members of the Money Industry Association arrive in Shanghai, a meeting will be held to discuss the matter in detail and present the reasons, so that a request can be made to the Legislative Yuan to enact separate regulations.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Mediated the Pier Donation Issue Yesterday

▲ Both the Guest Merchants and the Cotton Cloth Industry Insisted

▲ The Meeting Ended Yesterday Without Results

The cotton cloth industry and the forwarding and customs declaration industry had a dispute over the pier donation issue, which had not been resolved for a long time. Yesterday, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce convened both parties and the guest merchants for the second mediation. The attendees included Chen Songyuan, Ke Ganchen, and Shi Jiumao representing the cotton cloth industry; Shi Zikun and Zhu Xiechen representing the customs declaration industry; Yang Junxin representing the Sichuanese guest merchants; Wang Bohua representing the Shandong guest merchants; Gan Zhizhang representing the Shandong guest merchants; and Ji Chunyi, Wang Xinpu, and Sun Jiechen representing the guest merchants from Andong, Yantai, and Harbin, a total of eleven people. Lu Qinghua, director of the Commercial Affairs Section, chaired the meeting, reported the purpose of convening the mediation, and read out the letters from the cotton cloth industry and the guest merchants, and then asked all parties to express their opinions so that a decision could be discussed. First, Chen Songyuan, a representative of the cotton cloth industry, reported, roughly saying that the transaction between our industry and the guest merchants has always been delivered in the factory in this port. After the goods leave the factory, their ownership already belongs to the guest merchants, so the responsibility for paying the pier donation cannot be borne by our industry. This can be proved by the car fare problem resolved by the Social Bureau's mediation last time. Because the ownership of the goods has been transferred to the guest merchants, the car fare from the factory to the pier must be borne by the guest merchants. The pier donation for goods that have left the factory and reached the pier cannot be included in the scope of the cotton cloth industry. Next, Sun Jiechen, a representative of the guest merchants, reported that the guest merchants in Shanghai distinguish goods into large packages and small packages. The pier donation and car fare have always been included in the large packages. If they are proposed to be calculated separately now, it is inconsistent with the usual practice, and the guest merchants cannot recognize it. Next, Shi Zikun, a representative of the forwarding and customs declaration industry, reported that the pier donation has always been included in the price of goods and cannot be included in the freight price. If it is proposed to be calculated separately now, the guest merchants will have no way to report the accounts, which is also true. It is better to include it in the price of goods for convenience. The chairman's opinion is that the mediation must not violate the principles of the Social Bureau's resolved decision, and the responsibility must be determined, and the facts must be compromised to seek convenience in handling. According to the previous decision of the Social Bureau's mediation of car fare and the transfer of ownership of goods, the responsibility for paying the pier donation naturally belongs to the guest merchants. However, due to the lack of manpower to handle business, the guest merchants may entrust the cotton cloth industry to handle the procedures for paying the donation. After the donation is paid, the guest merchants will return all the agency payment to the cotton cloth industry. In this way, there is no conflict in facts and theory. As for the calculation of including the pier donation in the price of goods, it violates the method of the car fare problem mediated by the Social Bureau last time and should not be adopted. Therefore, two methods were drafted: (1) The procedures for paying the pier donation may be entrusted to the cotton cloth industry by the guest merchants. (2) The responsibility for paying the donation belongs to the guest merchants, who must be responsible for returning the full amount and shall not be short. After these two points were raised, the cotton cloth industry, in view of the previous lesson of the car fare problem, although it had been resolved by mediation, the guest merchants had still not fulfilled the agreement. Therefore, the issue of guaranteeing the return of the代繳donation was immediately raised. At the same time, the guest merchants still adhered to the established view of large and small packages. Therefore, the opinions of both parties could not be approached, and the meeting ended without results.

Jianghai Customs Notice on Regulations for Berthing Fees for All Vessels

▲ Type A: 25 taels per day

Jianghai Customs, Shanghai Port Berths, has rented berths to Chinese and foreign shipping companies for mooring ships. The berthing fees set must be calculated for at least three days. Luo Fude, the Customs Commissioner of Jianghai Customs, specially issued a notice yesterday, saying that the previous lease price for shipping companies in this port to rent this Customs berth in Shanghai Port for mooring ships must be calculated for at least three days. From July 1 this year, it should be changed to one day. There is no change to the berthing fees charged per day. The various berthing fees are listed as follows: Type A berth: 25 taels of regular silver per day or less than one day; Type B berth: 17 taels of regular silver per day or less than one day; Type C berth: 21 taels of regular silver per day or less than one day.

The Vast Majority of Sailors and Seamen Have Been Dismissed

It has been two months since the China Merchants Bureau's Guangda ship stopped running. It was initially planned to sell it, but because the ship's employees opposed it, the ship was permanently suspended and planned to be dismantled and converted into a lighter. On the 16th, an order was issued to dismiss all crew members, stokers, and supervisors. The seafarers were each paid two months' salary. After this matter was announced, the employees expressed dissatisfaction, because it was not cost-effective to not repair and operate such an excellent ship, but to rent an outside ship for 96,000 yuan a year to compensate for the household rent. Moreover, stopping and dismantling the ship would cut off the livelihoods of more than a hundred people. Therefore, Jun Anhui, Che Defang, was publicly elected to go to the bureau to petition the director. For the sake of maintaining the lives of all workers, Mr. Che has been negotiating with the bureau for days. As a result, eleven stokers were retained to guard the ship. Yesterday, the Guangda was opened to Gaochangmiao for demolition. All the equipment of the supervisor part was completely abandoned, and the loss was the greatest.

The National Medical Community Discusses the Reform of Measurement Issues

The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau has decided to implement the new system of weights and measures from July 1. The implementation period is not far away. The Shanghai National Medical Association believes that the dosage of medicine is by no means comparable to general food products. If there are inconsistencies at the beginning of the promotion, whether it is too light or too heavy, it will have a huge impact on the patient's family. Without unified innovation, it is particularly difficult to use the dosage of traditional Chinese medicine prescriptions. Therefore, at 8:00 pm the night before, a joint meeting of the Shanghai National Medical and Pharmaceutical Circles was convened at the association's office to discuss the implementation methods. Representatives of the National Medical Association, Jiang Wenfang and Zhu Hegao, representatives of the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association, Zhang Meian and Zhuang Meitang, and others all believed that it is imperative to unify weights and measures in this city, and the pharmaceutical industry cannot be unique. However, if the initial reform is not unified and replaced, it will be particularly detrimental to the dosage of the medical community and the lives of patients. It was decided that the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association would first convene colleagues to determine the implementation date, and then notify the National Medical Association to inform all members to follow and change in order to unify and avoid delays.

The Candle Industry Complies with the Order to Use New Instruments

The Shanghai Candle Industry Association complied with the order to use new measuring instruments and notified all members yesterday, saying that the Social Bureau ordered that the new system of weights and measures be promoted in this city, and July 1 was set as the unified deadline. All old instruments will be invalidated by the end of June. The association decided to notify all members to comply with the order to promote it at the members' meeting on the 17th. Be sure to implement it within the time limit. The new instruments to be used are limited to being purchased from the Xiejiao Weights and Measures Inspection Office before July 1, or purchased from a scale shop. If they are found and punished after the deadline, they will be responsible for their own actions. The association cannot help it, and the fines are huge, so be sure to pay attention and do not neglect it.

Price Survey After the Implementation of the Market Catty

▲ Estimated Price Increase of One-Tenth

The new system of weights and measures in this city, the Social Bureau has received instructions from the Ministry of Industry, approving its advance implementation on July 1st, announcing the unified use. However, the scales in small vegetable markets will be subject to inspection starting June 1st, with personnel dispatched to ban the use of old scales and replace them with new ones. Previously, the scales in small vegetable markets were inconsistent, with 18 taels accounting for 60%, 20 taels accounting for 20%, and 22 or 24 taels accounting for 10%. Now, one market catty is equivalent to only 13 taels and 6 mace and 4 fen of the old scales. A reporter from Xin Sheng She believes that since the market catty is smaller than the previously used scales, there should be changes in prices. Yesterday, he went to various vendors in Tangjiawan, Ximen, to investigate. Before, one yuan could buy 2 catties of rooster, now one yuan can buy 2 catties and 2 taels. Before, one yuan could buy 1 catty and 10 taels of hen, now it's 2 catties. Before, one yuan could buy 2 catties and 12 taels of fresh meat, now it's still 2 catties and 12 taels. Before, beef cost 800 cash per catty, now it's 700 cash. Before, Japanese fish cost 520 cash per catty, now it's 480 cash. Before, cuttlefish cost 400 cash per catty, now it's 280 cash. Before, taro cost 140 cash per catty, now it's 120 cash. Before, salted vegetables cost 120 cash per catty, now it's 100 cash. Before, white radish cost 120 cash per catty, now it's 100 cash. Before, bean sprouts cost 140 cash per catty, now it's 120 cash. The price difference between before and after implementation is about 85%, but on average, prices have risen by about one-tenth.

Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau Completes the Unification of City Power Plants

▲First Step of the Plan

Since the Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau established the plan to unify the city's power plants, it has been proceeding step by step according to the established procedures. The first step is to require all small power plants that need to expand their equipment in the future to change their approach and connect their power lines to the nearest large power plant, purchasing and reselling electricity from them. This first step of the plan was completely finished by May 1931. The progress is briefly described below:

The Zhenru Electric Company was the smallest electric company in the city, with a total capacity of only 46 KVA. Jinan University was its largest customer. In the summer of 1928, the university expanded its campus, and the number of lights increased sharply. The company's original equipment was insufficient to supply the demand. It originally planned to add machinery and expand its capacity, but after the bureau calculated it, it was not cost-effective, so it ordered it to negotiate with the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company to purchase electricity and instructed it on the engineering plan. After several contacts, the two parties agreed and signed a power supply contract on August 15, 1928. The power supply method was for the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company to install a 100 KVA open-air transformer at Dujiazhai, the border between Zhenru and Zhabei, to reduce the 6,600-volt voltage to 3,000 volts and then send it to Zhenru Town and the Zhenru Electric Plant in Yangjiaqiao. It also stipulated that the power supply capacity of Zhabei should be temporarily limited to 50 kilowatts. Zhenru paid Zhabei electricity bills at a minimum of 2,500 degrees per month, at a rate of 7 fen per degree. It began to supply electricity on October 1, 1928, which was the first step of the bureau's unification of the city's power plants. Subsequently, the two companies renewed the contract on December 31, 1929, changing the power supply capacity to a maximum of 70 kilowatts, with a minimum monthly power consumption of 4,000 degrees, at a rate of 8.3 cents per degree. At the beginning of the Zhenru Electric Company's purchase of electricity from the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, the transformer was installed at Dujiazhai, the border between Zhenru and Zhabei, as a place for electricity to be sent from Zhabei, which was originally for the convenience of the actual situation at the time, but the place was far from the company's power supply center, and the line loss was quite large. If it was damaged, repairs were also inconvenient. The bureau had long instructed the company to plan to move it. In the autumn of 1930, the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company supplied power to the International Communications Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications in front of the Jinwang Temple in Zhenru. The line started from the Ziyangqiao main substation in Zhabei, went northwest through the south of Pengpu Town, and then west to the Zhenru area, along Xincun Road, to near the Zhenru Electric Company, and then turned northwest along Taopu West Road to the radio station in front of the Jinwang Temple. This line can be greatly utilized, so it was decided to build another transformer station on the east side of the Jinan University junior high school dormitory. Jinan University is the largest customer of the Zhenru Electric Company, and most of the electricity supplied by the company is for the university, so the above location is actually the company's power supply center. Now this project is about to be completed and will soon be able to use this power supply method. After the Zhenru Electric Company implemented the bureau's plan and purchased electricity from the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, the next company was the Xianghua Electric Company. The Xianghua Company had four generators with a total capacity of 575 KVA. The population in its business area was dense, and the demand for electricity was increasing day by day. Moreover, with the establishment of factories, the demand for power was even greater. In August 1929, it was found that its maximum load had reached 396 kilowatts, which was almost the same as the total capacity of the entire plant. According to the historical increase ratio, it was estimated that its maximum load would soon be above 500 kilowatts. If it did not quickly plan to expand, it would not be able to cope. At that time, the Zhabei Yongdian Company already had a 6,600-volt high-voltage power line to the Xiangyanqiao bank on the Shajing Port, and the area east of the Shajing Port was the business area of the Xianghua Company, which was very close and convenient for electrification. Therefore, the company was ordered to negotiate with the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company on power supply methods. After the two companies negotiated, they signed a power supply contract on November 30, 1929, which was implemented from January 1930. The power supply capacity of Zhabei was temporarily limited to 600 kilowatts. The electricity price was divided into basic and floating parts. The basic part was calculated at 3 taels, 1 mace, 2 fen, and 5 li of silver per kilowatt of maximum power consumption per month, and was adjusted appropriately according to the level of the load factor. The floating part was calculated at 1 fen of silver per degree, and was appropriately increased or decreased according to the amount of heat required for each degree of power generation and the level of coal prices. The power supply method was to extend a 6,600-volt high-voltage power line from the Xiangyanqiao bank into the Xianghua area and distribute it to the Tianbao Road and Wuhua Road substations, reducing it to low voltage to supply users. Now, in view of the fact that this power supply method is not yet perfect, it is being planned to improve it. (To be continued)

Continued Trial of Battery Counterfeiting Case

▲ Trademark Has No Factual Basis

▲ Manufacturing Method Needs Investigation

Hu Guoguang of the China Storage Battery Factory accused Ding XiongZhao and He Cai, the owners of the Huiming Battery Factory, of counterfeiting the Fifth Thirty Brand battery trademark. The French Concession Court summoned them again yesterday. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that the plaintiff had purchased half a dozen "Da Wu Wei" brand flashlights produced by the defendant's factory from Kangfu Electrical Materials Factory. The trademark packaging paper stated that it was made of starch, which clearly showed that they were counterfeiting the plaintiff's trademark. The defendant's lawyer, Bian Jialu, argued that the plaintiff was instructed to provide evidence of counterfeiting last time. In today's court hearing, the plaintiff did not present any evidence, only claimed that the defendant was counterfeiting the plaintiff's manufacturing method. After investigation, the manufacturing methods of both parties are different, and chemists can be invited to study them. As for the "Da Wu Wei" brand products produced by the defendant's factory, both the material and value comparison are above the "Fifth Thirty Brand." There is no reason to counterfeit its trademark. Judge Zhu Chen issued a ruling that this case needs to be divided into two points: (1) whether the defendant counterfeited the trademark; (2) whether the manufacturing methods are the same. Today, it was found that there is no factual basis for the counterfeiting of the trademark. The manufacturing method will be investigated and verified after the witnesses are summoned.

Suicide Due to Lack of Funds for Marriage

▲ Sun Yongfu Is Also Pitiful

Sun Yongfu, a native of Shandong, is 30 years old and works as a male servant at the Lin Pinsun's home at 35 Foch Lane, Foch Road, French Concession. He has not yet married. He was engaged to a woman surnamed Xu, also from his hometown, in his hometown. Because Sun was working in Shanghai and had a very small income, he had no money to return to his hometown to get married. He has been wasting time until now. Counting the years, he suddenly received a letter from his family urging him to return home to complete the marriage. Sun thought that he had no savings in his hand, and there was no prospect for the wedding money and the cost of the banquet. Even after the marriage, the living expenses of the two people would be difficult to maintain. If he did not return home, the man and woman would be grown up and should be married. He would inevitably be questioned by the woman's family. He had no face to see the elders in his hometown. There was no fun in life, and he suddenly had the idea of suicide. On the afternoon of the 16th of this month, he secretly went to the Hongkou Grand Hotel on North Sichuan Road, booked room number 30, paid the room fee first, and then went out to buy two yuan of opium paste. He returned to the hotel, closed the door and went to bed, secretly swallowing it. He slept until 12 noon the next day. The hotel tea servant Zhuang Yuebin saw that the guest in room number 30 had not yet gotten up. According to the hotel regulations, after 12 o'clock, he would have to pay the room fee for one more day, so the tea room knocked on the door, intending to ask if he would continue to rent it. Unexpectedly, he knocked for a long time without response. He knew something was wrong, so he tried to open the door and enter the room. He saw Sun lying stiffly in bed, moaning non-stop. He immediately informed the accountant and reported it to the Hongkou Patrol Station. The patrol station ordered detectives to go to the hotel to inquire about Sun's situation. He was immediately taken to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. However, because he had been poisoned deeply, he died at 6 AM yesterday. The body has already been taken to the Fei Lun Road examination room for examination.

▲Rickshaw Industry: The Rickshaw Industry Association issued a message urging fellow members to continue to unite, stating that the association has been established for nearly four years. During these four years, it has strived for internal unity and the elimination of long-standing malpractices. However, eliminating malpractices is more difficult than promoting benefits, so all public welfare undertakings that should have been carried out have not been fully realized, which the association deeply regrets. Over the past four years, thanks to the concerted efforts and mutual understanding of fellow members, the following can be reported: (1) Reduced frequency of vehicle inspections: The Public Works Bureau inspected vehicles quarterly, four times a year, which, after repeated requests from the association, was reduced to three times. The inspection notices are also distributed evenly by the association based on time, distance, and the number of vehicles. This provides some convenience for vehicle owners and the Vehicle Affairs Office. (2) Gradual elimination of rickshaw thieves: Rickshaw theft and extortion have harmed rickshaw pullers and affected the business of rickshaw dealers, causing deep resentment among industry members for more than a day or two. Since the association petitioned the Public Security Bureau to send the main culprits to the Caohéjing vagrant work-study center, while rickshaw theft in the Chinese area has not been completely eliminated, it is no longer as blatant and unconcerned as before. (3) The French Concession withdrew its order to increase license fees and restrict licenses: The monthly license fees for vehicles operating in the French Concession were determined by the number of rickshaw pullers. Subsequently, the Municipal Council proposed increasing license fees and restricting licenses, changing the old system. After the association jointly demanded this with rickshaw dealers in the Public Concession, the order was withdrawn. To this day, one vehicle still has one license and is not subject to any restrictions. The above are just a few examples that everyone knows. The future is long, and what rickshaw dealers hope for from the association and what the association wants to strive for on behalf of rickshaw dealers are not limited to these few points. Without the joint efforts of rickshaw dealers, how can we obtain the protection of the government, how can we alleviate the suffering of rickshaw pullers, and how can we break free from the shackles of imperialism? Four years of unity have yielded such barely satisfactory results. If we add the 10,000 vehicles in the Public Concession, which have also joined the association, the future status of the association will be beyond imagination. It all depends on the efforts of the rickshaw industry. Currently, the 1,477 vehicles newly released by the Public Works Bureau have not yet fully joined the association's insurance scheme. The association believes that a sound organization is closely related to the rickshaw industry and humbly presents these considerations for your understanding.

▲Fruit Industry: The Fruit and Native Produce Industry Association has a standing Economic Management Committee consisting of five elected members who manage the association's financial affairs. All deposits and withdrawals in banks and money houses must be stamped by these committee members. The previous committee members, Zhang Zhuxi, Xu Xianchang, and others, have completed their terms. The election of the new Economic Management Committee was held the other day. The election was held at 2:00 PM, and the ballot box results showed that Cai Runsen, Cheng Xueshi, Chen Jianfu, Wang Guosheng, and Dong Chunxue were elected. They took office on the spot. Subsequently, the association sent letters to the banks and money houses it deals with, along with the specimen signatures of the five new committee members. Henceforth, all deposits and withdrawals must be stamped by the committee members to ensure prudence.

▲Silk and Satin Industry: The Silk and Satin Industry Association held its 22nd Executive Committee meeting the other day. More than ten committee members attended, with Lu Zhengbing presiding. After formal greetings, the following resolutions were passed: (1) A letter from member Heng Huiji stated that Jilin Tiantaiheng owed money for goods and had repeatedly failed to respond to催促. It was resolved to forward the letter. (2) Omitted. (3) A letter from the Shantou Silk and Satin Cloth Industry Association requested the promotion of national goods and the cessation of foreign goods, instructing the association to collect and send the trademarks of its members' products to Shantou for customers to choose from. It was resolved to send separate letters to each guild to comply. (4) A letter from the Hankou Silk and Satin Industry Association proposed that the government should follow the example of foreign goods and impose a unified tax on domestically produced silk and satin to facilitate sales. The letter included a draft petition, instructing the association to distribute it to various merchant guilds in the inland areas for unanimous response. It was resolved to comply. (5) A letter from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce stated that the municipal government had allocated funds to prepare for the establishment of a manufacturing plant for new metric instruments, instructing the association to list the types and quantities of new instruments needed by a specific date for collection and use. It was resolved to notify all members, based on the report of Committee Member Jiang Linshu, to submit the list to the association by the 25th of this month for collection. (7) A letter from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce stated that the National Tariff Commission planned to hire personnel familiar with the industry's business and tariffs for research. (8) The association's general membership meeting is scheduled to be held annually in mid-June according to the articles of association. As the date is approaching, a date should be determined. Local News Two

New Drug Stores Should Exercise Caution When Selling Sleeping Pills

▲Five Measures for Prohibition

▲All Businesses Must Comply

The New Drug Stores Association yesterday copied and sent five measures to prohibit the sale of sleeping pills to all members, requesting strict compliance. They are recorded as follows: (1) Sleeping pills should not be sold to anyone who does not have a formal prescription signed by a doctor. (2) If there is no serious illness and a doctor has not prescribed a prescription, those purchasing a very small amount of sleeping pills must obtain a reliable guarantor to prove that they are indeed for treating an illness before they can be sold. (3) When drug stores sell sleeping pills, the bottle label and wrapper must have the drug store's name and the signature of the dispensing pharmacist, as well as the date. (4) When drug stores sell sleeping pills, they must ask for the purchaser's name, age, address, and doctor's name, and register them in detail for future reference. (5) Those purchasing sleeping pills with a formal doctor's prescription should only be sold the amount for one-time use and only valid for one time.

Chinese and British Buses Collide

丨On洋鎗小路丨

▲British Route 4 Bus Overturns

▲Four Men and Women Injured, Some Seriously

A British Public Bus Company Route 4 bus, running from Xujiahui to the airfield, collided with a Shanghai South Route 4 bus at 7:50 AM yesterday on洋鎗路, causing an accident. Four men and women were injured. The details of the accident are as follows:

▲Location of the Accident: Both the Shanghai South Public Bus Company Route 4 bus and the British Public Bus Route 4 bus operate from Xujiahui to the airfield. The two companies have fixed schedules and have never had any conflicts. Unexpectedly, at 7:50 AM yesterday, the Shanghai South Route 4 bus, driven by driver number 15 and with conductor number 24, was returning from Xujiahui to the airfield. When it reached麦根路, the British Route 4 bus was following closely behind at high speed. The bus, number 182 with driver number 182 and conductor number 117, was speeding up to try and get ahead and did not honk its horn. When it reached洋鎗小路, the road was narrow, and the side of the road was rugged and muddy, causing the wheels to get stuck in the mud. The Shanghai South Route 4 bus driver could not avoid it in time, and the two buses collided. With a loud crash, the entire British Route 4 bus overturned.

▲Four Injured: Fortunately, the accident occurred in the early morning, and there were few passengers. There were only four male passengers and one female passenger in the bus, as well as the driver and conductor, making a total of seven people. The driver of the bus, number 182, suffered a broken right foot, and the conductor, number 117, also suffered a serious injury to his right hand. One male passenger suffered a head injury, and one female passenger suffered a chest injury. After the accident, both bus companies used the phone to notify their respective companies to send people to the scene. The four injured people were sent to Shanghai Sanatorium for treatment. Whether their lives are safe is currently uncertain.

▲Company's Statement: Afterwards, a reporter visited Xia Shuxiang, the director of the Shanghai South Public Bus Company's Vehicle Affairs Department. According to him, the company's operations in that area have always been very stable, and both sides have fixed schedules and are not allowed to rush or overtake each other. This time, the company's bus was traveling ahead, and the British bus driver deliberately sped up to get ahead, causing the accident. The blame should be determined impartially by the authorities.

Qin Wenbin Admits to Stabbing Father Lang

▲Father Lang Refused to Write a Letter of Introduction

▲Qin Wenbin Acted Out of Extreme Hatred

The case of Qin Wenbin, a former cook at the Dongjiadu Catholic Church, stabbing Father Lang with a sharp knife on the night of the 15th of this month has been reported in previous newspapers. It is now known that after Qin Wenbin was sent to the Public Security Bureau, he was interrogated by the Third Section. Qin confessed that he was originally a cook at the church, but Father Zhang said he was lazy and fired him. He went to the震旦 University student village and asked Father Lang to write a letter of introduction, but he refused. He hated him so much that he went to the City God Temple to buy a sharp knife and stabbed him four times. The official asked if he killed him. He replied, "Yes." He was asked where he lived. He replied, "I live at my cousin Lu Qiusheng's house in Yangchang Alley, Xiaonanmen." On the night of the 15th, he entered through the garden of the church and stabbed Father Lang, who shouted in a foreign language. He then fled, throwing the knife in the garden. Because it was dark, no one saw him. After leaving, he went through Huozheng Lane to Yangchang Alley. His cousin was not awake, so he washed off the bloodstains. The next day, he took a boat back to his hometown in Nanhui, where he was arrested. After the section recorded his confession, it sent Qin to the District Court with a letter. After a preliminary hearing by the prosecutor, the defendant was ordered to be detained pending an examination of Father Lang's injuries before further proceedings.

Completion Date for the New Western Prison on Huade Road

▲Approximately One and a Half Years Later

▲Construction Cost of Two Million Taels

The number of inmates in the Western Prison on Huade Road has reached more than 5,000 in recent years. However, because the construction of the new prison next to the old prison is progressing rapidly, the crowded situation in the prison has been slightly reduced. The new prison building was originally laid in 1928. The estimated construction cost is more than two million taels. Most of it has now been built, but the entire project will not be completed for another year and a half. The site is approximately thirty acres and will have four prison buildings, one factory, one prison building for young prisoners, one prison hospital, one police hospital, one office for administrators, one dormitory for Indian police, and miscellaneous buildings. In the future, when the police hospital is completed, the existing hospital on Bazilu will be moved in. The new hospital can accommodate sixty-eight Indian police officers and one hundred and twenty-eight Chinese police officers. A separate prison hospital will be built, which can accommodate one hundred and forty-two patients. It will be connected to the police hospital by an underground passage. The four prison buildings are each five stories high and can accommodate four hundred and sixty prisoners each. They are constructed entirely of steel and reinforced concrete. The remaining offices and hospitals are each five to eight stories high.

Children's Hygiene Campaign Lantern Parade Yesterday

Yesterday was the opening day of the Children's Hygiene Campaign of the Ciyou Association. A lantern parade was held at 6:30 PM that evening. The details of yesterday are as follows:

▲A Glimpse of the Display: The Ciyou Health Clinic and Medical Center, set up by the Ciyou Association near the Guanyin Temple on Xiqiujiang Road in Zhabei, was filled with children's new clothes, shoes, hats, and other children's toys and foods, all produced by new-style stores in the city. Health forms, pictures, and slogans lined the walls. Although the building was narrow, the layout was quite good. Citizens who visited in the afternoon came in an endless stream.

▲Hygiene Work: From 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM yesterday, a children's health competition was held. A total of sixty-five children participated. Doctors Dang Wenshou and others examined the entire bodies of the children, and the results will be announced in a table soon. From 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM in the afternoon, three doctors from the Health Bureau administered vaccinations to adults and children in front of the Ciyou Health Clinic and Medical Center, totaling 345 people. The children's bathing was presided over by Ms. Hua Jingzhen and Hua Meijie. There were as many as thirty-seven people who were bathed. ▲Opening Performance: At six o'clock in the evening, representatives from the Municipal Party Committee, the Social Affairs Bureau, the Public Works Bureau, the Public Security Bureau, and the Health Bureau arrived one after another. The opening ceremony was then held. Wu Weide of the Ciyou Association reported the significance of holding the children's hygiene campaign. The representative of the Health Bureau spoke about the key points of children's hygiene. Then, the Juvenile Propaganda Team performed a costumed hygiene play, and the students of the Ciyou Education Institute performed a new play. From 10:00 PM to 11:00 PM, hygiene films were shown on-site.

▲Parade Situation: Yesterday was a day of continuous drizzle, but the sky gradually cleared in the evening. A total of five hundred and several dozen children from various schools participated. After six o'clock, they gathered on the grassland opposite the Guanyin Temple on Xiqiujiang Road. The orphanage's band was arranged in the front, and the other school children held red and green lanterns, or square lanterns with slogans, and model lanterns of mosquitoes and flies. The parade set off from Xiqiujiang Road, heading east and circling the planned routes. The lanterns shone brightly, and the entire team meandered like a long snake. After about an hour and a half, they returned to the original place and disbanded.

Truck Kills a Person

▲The Blame Lies with the Driver

▲Serious Punishment Ordered

Motorist Jiang Asi drove a truck on Haige Road in the French Concession on the afternoon of the 10th of this month. Due to the driver's negligence, he hit and killed a small cart puller, Zhang Loufu. The corpse was verified by the presiding judge. Yesterday, the police sent Jiang to the French court for questioning. The plaintiff, the corpse's family member Zhang Yangshi, extended律师律师 Beck to represent them, stating, "Our lawyer has found that there have been as many as seventeen cases of car accidents causing death in this concession this year, of which truck accidents account for three-tenths, indicating that most truck drivers deliberately neglect their duties. This case was also caused by the defendant driver's negligence, which has been proven by the police to be true. The deceased was fifty-two years old this year and had a wife and children, a total of five people, all of whom depended on the deceased for their livelihood. Now that he has been killed, the entire family has no means of support. We request compensation of five thousand taels." When questioned, the defendant Jiang Asi admitted that he was negligent and caused the accident and begged for leniency. The Chinese and Western judges sentenced Jiang to a fine of fifty yuan to be confiscated and ordered him to compensate the plaintiff's family with two thousand five hundred yuan. The truck was allowed to be temporarily detained. If the payment cannot be made, the truck will be auctioned off after July 10th to cover the amount.

Unfilial Son Beats His Mother

▲Spectators Greatly Outraged

▲Then Bowed His Head and Begged for Leniency

Liu Zhengfu from Jiangbei, forty-six years old, operates a flatbread shop at the western end of Songxing Road in Wusong. His son, Liu Dazhen, twenty-six years old, works in a flatbread shop behind the Huafeng Yarn Factory. The other day, after an argument with his wife, he beat his wife. Yesterday, Dazhen went to his father's flatbread shop and asked his mother, Liu Wangshi, forty-five years old, for money to treat his wife's injuries. His mother initially refused, but Dazhen smashed his own head with a stone. Seeing this, his mother gave him one yuan and told him to go home and treat his wife's injuries. Unexpectedly, Dazhen took the money and came back, arguing with his mother and raising the stone mill, throwing it at his mother's head. Fortunately, the spectators blocked it, preventing her from being injured. However, the unfilial son still did not give up, causing the spectators to feel outraged and want to beat him. The unfilial son, knowing that he had offended the public and fearing unfavorable consequences, jumped into the river to avoid it. The watchman of the first station of the seventh district happened to see this and rescued him, taking him to the station to report. After questioning by Zhang Jiguang, the head of the first station of the seventh district, the unfilial son bowed his head and begged for leniency, saying that he was willing to change his ways and would never commit such an act again. Director Zhang observed that Liu Wangshi was not injured and leniently sentenced him to three days of detention as a slight punishment.

Du Yuwei Walks to Kaifeng

Du Yuwei, a young man traveling alone on foot, set off from Kunshan in the summer of the eighteenth year, walking along the Shanghai-Hangzhou line into Zhejiang and Fujian, then to Guangdong and Guangxi, around Wuzhou. He then suffered from malaria in Guangdong and had to return to the capital to recuperate. After recovering from his illness, he mustered his courage and followed the Beijing-Shanghai line straight into Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan. At that time, due to the rampant communist bandits, he was unable to move forward. He transferred to the Jiaoji Railway, entering Qingzhou from Jiaozhou, reaching Jinan and then Caozhou. Along the way, Party, government, and academic circles warmly welcomed him, presenting him with many silk banners and holding meetings to invite him to give speeches, promoting customs and Party-oriented views. Mr. Du carried a camera with him and took pictures of all the famous scenic spots he passed through, in order to compile a walking special edition of field photographs in the future. Previously, due to climbing mountains and crossing rivers, his feet and thighs were exposed to moisture, resulting in sores. After receiving surgical treatment at Caozhou Hospital, he has now set off for Kaifeng.
